 unhone aashaa jataai he ki isse bhartiya arthvyavastha do pratishat kii vruddhi ke saath asia kii teesri sabase badi arthvyavastha ban jaaegi
 5) Government is of the opinion that GST will make the functioning of industries easier
 isamen pratispardhaa ke saath rajyon main nirmaan ko protsaahan milegaa

 6
 Experts, on the other hand, say that in the states concerned with losing revenue in many areas, the GST proposal includes several agreements

 The young man died of cancer
 lekin police ke dakhal dene par parijan laash lekar kahin or chale gaye

 jisaki umr kareeb 17 varsh thi
 a few days ago, the young man was admitted to a government hospital in Mumbai due to cancer
 ilaj ke dauraan beeti 27 oktober ko uski maut ho gai thi
 After this, the youth's family was surrounded by superstition that the young man would be alive again
 isi ke chalate ek carch main use jinda karne ke liye vishesh prarthana shuru hui
 But the police knew about this
 police ne mritak ke parivaar waalon ko notice jari kar diya
